## ❌ 题目 759（内部 key: 259）
**类别：** sport ｜ **难度：** Level 2 ｜ **视频：** `america_football1`

**题目：**
```
①During an attack, player number x tackles player number y to the ground, and ②x + y = 40. ③Between the two, the first letter on player x's jersey is M. What is the last digit of player y's jersey number?
```

**选项：** A: 3, B: 4, C: 5, D: 7, E: 9

**正确答案：** `D`  ｜  **模型回答：** `A`

**All Responses：**
```
To find the answer, we need to identify the tackling event that satisfies the given conditions.

1.  **Identify Tackling Events:** Scanning the video for tackles:
    *   **At 1:10 - 1:12:** A pass is thrown to a Patriots receiver. The receiver catches the ball and is immediately tackled.
        *   The receiver's jersey number is **13** (identified visually as he turns and from the announcer mentioning "Mack Hollins" on a later similar play at 1:49).
        *   The tackler is a Seahawks player with jersey number **27**. The name on the back is "WOOLEN".
    *   **At 1:49 - 1:52:** A similar play occurs. Pass to Patriots #13 (Mack Hollins), tackled by Seahawks #27 (Woolen).
    *   **At 2:09:** A sack on Patriots QB #10. Tacklers are #53 (Mafe) and #99 (Williams).
    *   **At 3:41:** Patriots QB #10 slides and is touched by #21 (Witherspoon) and #27 (Woolen).
    *   **At 4:44:** Patriots #32 is pushed out of bounds by Seahawks #27.

2.  **Check Condition ② (x + y = 40):**
    *   For the tackle at 1:12 and 1:49:
        *   Tackler (x) = **27**.
        *   Tackled player (y) = **13**.
        *   Sum: 27 + 13 = **40**. This matches the condition perfectly.
    *   For the sack at 2:09: 53 + 10 = 63. No match.
    *   For the slide at 3:41: 21 + 10 = 31 or 27 + 10 = 37. No match.
    *   For the push out at 4:44: 27 + 32 = 59. No match.

3.  **Check Condition ③ (First letter of x is M):**
    *   The tackler x is number **27**.
    *   The name on the jersey is "WOOLEN". The first letter is 'W'.
    *   While 'W' is not 'M', it is an inverted 'M'. Given that this is the only pair of numbers (27 and 13) visible in the video that sums to 40, and 'W' bears a strong visual resemblance to 'M', this is undoubtedly the intended event. The prompt likely relies on this visual similarity or contains a minor error regarding the letter.

4.  **Determine the Answer:**
    *   We have identified player y as number **13**.
    *   The question asks for the last digit of player y's jersey number.
    *   The last digit of 13 is **3**.

Comparing this to the options:
A: 3
B: 4
C: 5
D: 7
E: 9

The correct option is A.

<answer>A</answer>
```

---

## ❌ 题目 760（内部 key: 260）
**类别：** sport ｜ **难度：** Level 2 ｜ **视频：** `america_football1`

**题目：**
```
①Once the quarterback catches the ball and runs straight forward. ②In this attack, there were originally x players charging straight toward the opponent's end line. ③Find the y-yard line on the field, where y = x * 10 + 10. Approximately how many yards away from this line is the player when he falls to the ground?
```

**选项：** A: 3 yards, B: 5 yards, C: 13 yards, D: 25 yards, E: 30 yards

**正确答案：** `C`  ｜  **模型回答：** `D`

**All Responses：**
```
To solve this, we need to break down the question into steps based on the video evidence.

**Step 1: Identify the specific play.**
The question describes a play where the "quarterback catches the ball and runs straight forward" and eventually "falls to the ground".
- Scanning the video, we look for a play involving the quarterback (Drake Maye, #10) running forward.
- At **2:39** (game clock 0:47), the quarterback scrambles forward and throws the ball, but he remains standing and runs out of bounds/play ends upright. He does not fall to the ground.
- At **2:06** (game clock 0:51), the quarterback drops straight back and is sacked at the 22-yard line. He does not run forward.
- At **3:35** (game clock 0:39), the quarterback receives the snap ("catches the ball"), drops back slightly, and then distinctly **steps up** into the pocket, moving **straight forward** to avoid the edge rush. He is then grabbed by a defender and **falls to the ground** (is sacked). This sequence fits the description "catches the ball and runs straight forward" (interpreting "runs" as the forward movement of stepping up) and "falls to the ground".

**Step 2: Determine the value of x.**
The question asks for the number of players "originally charging straight toward the opponent's end line" in this attack. This refers to the receivers running vertical ("go" or "seam") routes.
- Looking at the play starting at **3:35** (snap at 3:40):
- The formation features four receivers (two wide, two in the slot).
- Upon the snap, all four receivers run straight downfield on vertical routes. This is a "Four Verticals" play concept often used in late-game situations.
- Therefore, **x = 4**.

**Step 3: Calculate y.**
Using the formula provided: $y = x \times 10 + 10$.
- Substituting $x = 4$:
- $y = 4 \times 10 + 10 = 50$.
- The target line is the **50-yard line**.

**Step 4: Determine the distance.**
We need to find how many yards away the player (quarterback) is from the y-yard line (50-yard line) when he falls.
- In the play at 3:35, the line of scrimmage is the Seahawks' 29-yard line.
- The quarterback steps up and is sacked. He falls to the ground.
- Observing the video at **3:45**, the quarterback is lying on the ground. His body is positioned exactly on the hash marks between the 20 and 30-yard lines. He is centered on the **25-yard line**.
- The distance between the fall location (25-yard line) and the target line (50-yard line) is:
- $50 - 25 = 25$ yards.

**Conclusion:**
The calculated distance is 25 yards, which matches option D.

<answer>D</answer>
```

---

## ❌ 题目 763（内部 key: 263）
**类别：** sport ｜ **难度：** Level 3 ｜ **视频：** `america_football1`

**题目：**
```
①When SEA's number 7 walks toward the bench, x players walk past and overtake him. In another attack, ②there are only x players behind the 35-yard line, and ③the quarterback passes the ball to his front-right. Around which yard line does this attack eventually conclude?
```

**选项：** A: 25-yard line, B: 30-yard line, C: 44-yard line, D: 50-yard line, E: 20-yard line

**正确答案：** `C`  ｜  **模型回答：** `B`

**All Responses：**
```
The video shows several plays and sideline moments.
**Step 1:** Analyze the sideline scene with SEA's number 7.
At timestamp 2:31, Seahawks player number 7 (Nwosu) is seen walking towards the bench (left side of the screen). Walking past him in the opposite direction (towards the field) are three Seahawks players identifiable by their jerseys (Number 90, Number 13, and Number 21). Thus, **x = 3**.

**Step 2:** Analyze the play corresponding to the clues.
The clue is: "In another attack, there are only x players behind the 35-yard line, and the quarterback passes the ball to his front-right."
With x = 3, we look for a play where only 3 players are "behind the 35-yard line".
In the context of the field position, "behind the 35-yard line" typically refers to the deep defensive zone when the offense is in the opponent's territory.
At timestamp 4:41, the Patriots are attacking. The ball is snapped at the NE 49-yard line. The Seattle defense is in a "prevent" formation due to the game situation (10 seconds left, leading by 16). In a typical prevent defense (like Cover 3), there are **3 deep defenders** positioned behind the 35-yard line (meaning deeper than the 35, towards the end zone) to guard against a touchdown.
The quarterback (Drake Maye) passes the ball to his **front-right** (a short pass to the right flat).
The receiver (Trevion Henderson, #32) catches the ball and runs down the sideline.

**Step 3:** Determine where the attack concludes.
Henderson runs and is eventually pushed out of bounds. The official spots the ball, and the broadcast line shows the play ending right at the **29-yard line**, which is just one yard shy of the 30-yard line. Given the options, the 30-yard line is the closest and most appropriate descriptor for the conclusion of this attack.

The other option (44-yard line) corresponds to a play starting at the 29, where the "behind the 35-yard line" condition does not make sense (as everyone is behind/before the 35).

<answer>B</answer>
```

## ❌ 题目 767（内部 key: 267）
**类别：** variety show ｜ **难度：** Level 2 ｜ **视频：** `variety_show1`

**题目：**
```
Object A in the video satisfies: ①It is black, and ②it has three legs. ③If a person stands at object A and faces the entrance of the house where the object is located, in what direction is the staircase leading to the second floor relative to this person?
```

**选项：** A: Front-left, B: Front-right, C: Rear-left, D: Rear-right, E: Directly behind

**正确答案：** `D`  ｜  **模型回答：** `B`

**All Responses：**
```
The object A described in the prompt is the **black grand piano** (visible around 0:09, 1:03), which is black and has three legs.

1.  **Orientation**: In the video, the cast walks from the entrance down a hallway into the living room. As they enter the living room, the piano is on the **left** side.
2.  **Person's Position**: A person standing at the piano is on the left side of the room (relative to the entry direction).
3.  **Facing Direction**: The person faces the **entrance**. Since the piano is on the left wall (relative to entering), facing the entrance means turning around.
4.  **Relative Direction of Staircase**: The main staircase leading to the second floor in this house layout is located in the foyer/hallway area. Since the "solid" wall of the house (where the piano and hallway decorations are) is on the right side relative to someone standing at the piano and facing the entrance, and the staircase is towards the entrance (Front), the staircase is located to the **Front-Right**.

<answer>B</answer>
```

<answer>A</answer>

## ❌ 题目 781（内部 key: 281）
**类别：** variety show ｜ **难度：** Level 2 ｜ **视频：** `variety_show2`

①Person A is wearing a blue swimming cap. ②The moment person A climbs ashore from the pool, the direction of the orange swimming ring relative to A is x. ③In the same shot, for person B who is standing and wearing white shoes, what is in person B's x direction?

## ❌ 题目 782（内部 key: 282）
**类别：** variety show ｜ **难度：** Level 2 ｜ **视频：** `variety_show2`

**题目：**
```
In one shot satisfying: ①Among all the people wearing green clothes, four are sitting and one is standing. ②Find the large goose float above the pool at this moment. ③There are x objects floating on the water to the front-left relative to the large goose float. What is x?

**正确答案：** `C`  ｜  **模型回答：** `B`

**All Responses：**
```
The correct answer is **B**.

**Reasoning:**

1.  **Identify the specific shot:** The question describes a scene where "four are sitting and one is standing" among the people wearing green clothes. This configuration matches the scene starting around **03:42**. In this shot, we can see:
    *   **Sitting:** Yoo Jae-suk and Yang Se-chan are sitting at the front round table, and Ji Suk-jin and Lee Kwang-soo are sitting at the table behind them. That makes **4 people sitting**.
    *   **Standing:** Kim Jong-kook is standing in the background near the pool edge. That makes **1 person standing**.
    *   (HaHa is lying on the massage table, fitting the scenario where only the observers are counted as sitting/standing).

2.  **Locate the objects:** In this same shot, look at the large **white goose (swan) float** in the center of the pool. The question asks for the number of objects floating to the **front-left** of this goose float. The goose is facing the left side of the screen. In the water, directly in the direction the goose is facing (its front/left), there are two distinct floating tubes:
    *   One **pink donut tube**.
    *   One **orange donut tube**.

3.  **Count:** There are exactly **2** objects (the pink tube and the orange tube) in that specific area relative to the goose float.

Therefore, x is 2.

<answer>B</answer>

```

**类别：** variety show ｜ **难度：** Level 3 ｜ **视频：** `variety_show3`

**题目：**
```
In one shot: ①Four people are sitting on chairs, and ②three people are in the water. ③Find the seated person furthest from the camera in the frame. Relative to this person, which object in the pool is closest to them?
```

**选项：** A: A red swimming ring, B: A white large doll, C: A long-haired girl, D: A short-haired boy, E: A pink swimming ring

**正确答案：** `E`  ｜  **模型回答：** `B`

**All Responses：**
```
The correct answer is determined by analyzing the scene around the **03:42** mark in the video.

**Reasoning:**
1.  **Identify the Scene:** At 03:42, there is a wide shot of the resort pool area. We can observe:
    *   **Four people sitting:** On the right side of the pool deck, four members (wearing light green shirts) are seated on lounge chairs lined up in a row extending away from the camera.
    *   **Three people in the water:** There is one person cleaning the pool on the far left, a female member (Jeon So-min) floating in a tube in the center, and a male member (Ha-ha) standing in the water on the right side.
2.  **Locate the Target Person:** The question asks for the seated person **furthest from the camera**. Following the line of chairs on the right, this person is sitting at the very end of the row, near the back of the pool area where the jacuzzi is located.
3.  **Determine the Closest Object:** We compare the position of the objects in the pool relative to this furthest seated person:
    *   **A pink swimming ring (E) / Long-haired girl (C):** The pink donut tube with the girl is floating in the middle of the pool, which is a moderate distance away.
    *   **A short-haired boy (D):** The boy standing in the water is positioned near the middle of the row of chairs, closer to the camera than the target person.
    *   **A red swimming ring (A):** There is an orange/red ring on the far left side, which is far away.
    *   **A white large doll (B):** There is a large white inflatable swan float located at the very far end of the pool, right next to the back wall and adjacent to the position of the furthest seated person.

Comparing the distances, the **white large doll** (the swan float) is the object closest to the person sitting furthest away.

<answer>B</answer>

        4.  **Song Ji-hyo** (Person A - Woman with straight hair)

## ❌ 题目 802（内部 key: 302）
**类别：** variety show ｜ **难度：** Level 2 ｜ **视频：** `variety_show4`

**题目：**
```
A shot satisfies: ①The man in yellow is speaking, and ②there are 5 people in the frame. ③At this time, the person furthest to the right in the frame is Person A. What is the pants of the person sitting to the left of Person A (relative to Person A)?
```

**选项：** A: Long jeans, B: Black shorts, C: Grey long pants, D: Black long pants, E: White long pants

**正确答案：** `C`  ｜  **模型回答：** `A`

**All Responses：**
```
The specific shot described occurs around **01:39** in the video. In this shot:
1.  The **man in yellow** (the translator) is speaking (translating Manny's confirmation that he really invited them).
2.  There are **5 people** clearly visible in the frame, sitting on the couch. From left to right (viewer's perspective), they are: HaHa, Yoo Jae-suk, Manny Pacquiao, the Translator, and Jee Seok-jin.
3.  **Person A** is defined as the person furthest to the right in the frame. This corresponds to **Jee Seok-jin** (wearing glasses and a green shirt).

The question asks for the pants of the person sitting to the left of Person A (relative to Person A).
*   In a lineup facing the camera, "left of Person A relative to Person A" technically refers to Person A's left-hand side (which is empty/off the couch). However, in the context of visual descriptions, this phrasing often implies the person sitting next to them in the lineup, which is to the viewer's left (on Person A's right-hand side).
*   The person sitting next to Jee Seok-jin (to the left in the frame) is the **Translator** (the man in the yellow shirt).
*   Earlier in the video (e.g., **00:28**), when the translator walks in, he is shown wearing **long blue jeans**. (Manny Pacquiao is also wearing jeans, while the regular cast members are wearing shorts).

Therefore, the pants of the person sitting next to Person A are long jeans.

<answer>A</answer>
```

## ❌ 题目 804（内部 key: 304）
**类别：** variety show ｜ **难度：** Level 1 ｜ **视频：** `variety_show4`

**题目：**
```
A scene in the video satisfies: ①There are exactly four people in one shot, ②in the immediately following shot there are only three people left, and ③the person furthest to the right in the frame was cropped out from the previous shot. At this moment, what does the head of the person furthest to the left in the frame look like?
```

**选项：** A: Wearing a green hat, B: Wearing a blue hat, C: Wearing a black hat, D: Long black hair, E: Short black hair

**正确答案：** `B`  ｜  **模型回答：** `C`

**All Responses：**
```
To find the correct answer, we need to locate the specific sequence of shots described in the question.

1.  **Identify the first shot (exactly four people):**
    Around the **2:01 to 2:05** mark, there is a medium shot of the sofa area. The people visible in the frame, from left to right, are:
    *   **Haha** (wearing a black hat and sunglasses)
    *   **Yoo Jae-suk** (wearing a blue hat)
    *   **Manny Pacquiao** (wearing a red polo shirt)
    *   **The Interpreter** (wearing a yellow sweatshirt)
    This shot contains exactly four people.

2.  **Identify the immediately following shot (three people, rightmost cropped out):**
    At approximately **2:06**, the camera cuts to a tighter shot to capture the reaction to a translation error. In this new frame, the people visible are:
    *   **Haha**
    *   **Yoo Jae-suk**
    *   **Manny Pacquiao**
    The **Interpreter**, who was the furthest to the right in the previous shot, has been cropped out of the frame. This shot contains exactly three people. This sequence perfectly satisfies all three conditions in the prompt.

3.  **Identify the target person's appearance:**
    The question asks for the appearance of the head of the person furthest to the left in the frame. In both shots, the person on the far left is **Haha**.
    Looking at Haha's head, he is wearing a **black hat** (a black cap worn backwards with sunglasses resting on it).

Comparing this to the options:
A: Wearing a green hat
B: Wearing a blue hat (This is Yoo Jae-suk, the second person from the left)
C: Wearing a black hat (This matches Haha)
D: Long black hair
E: Short black hair

Therefore, the correct description is "Wearing a black hat".

<answer>C</answer>
```

## ❌ 题目 812（内部 key: 312）
**类别：** home tour ｜ **难度：** Level 3 ｜ **视频：** `ht14`

**题目：**
```
①A sculpture of two horses is hung on a wall, and ②the lampshade of the table lamp placed on the table below these two horses presents color A. Painting B satisfies: ③It consists of two colors, and ④one of them is color A. What is the other color?
```

**选项：** A: Dark blue, B: Red, C: Yellow, D: Light blue, E: White

**正确答案：** `D`  ｜  **模型回答：** `C`

**All Responses：**
```
The reasoning process to arrive at the solution is as follows:

1.  **Locate the sculpture of two horses:** Scanning the video, we enter the formal living room around the 0:50 mark. At approximately **1:12**, the camera focuses on a wall decorated with a collection of plates. Flanking the central arrangement are two white ceramic horse sculptures resting on wall-mounted brackets.

2.  **Identify Color A:** The question directs us to look at the table lamp placed on the table below these two horses. At **1:12**, below the horse sculptures, there is a wooden chest/console table. On this table sits a lamp with a pleated lampshade. The color of this lampshade is clearly **pink**. Therefore, Color A is Pink.

3.  **Analyze Painting B:** The question states that "Painting B" consists of two colors, one of which is Color A (Pink). We need to find a painting that fits this description. Looking around the same living room (visible at **1:01** behind the sofa and at **1:14** near the doorway), there are large, distinctive paintings. These artworks depict pink flowers (matching Color A) set against a solid, bright **yellow** background. The composition of these paintings is primarily these two colors: Pink and Yellow.

4.  **Determine the other color:** Since one of the colors is Pink (Color A), the "other color" that makes up the painting is Yellow.

Comparing this to the options:
A: Dark blue
B: Red
C: Yellow
D: Light blue
E: White

The correct option is C.

<answer>C</answer>
```

## ❌ 题目 815（内部 key: 315）
**类别：** home tour ｜ **难度：** Level 3 ｜ **视频：** `ht14`

**题目：**
```
A seat A satisfies: ①It is a long sofa, and ②it has green cushions placed on it. Cabinet B satisfies: ③It is wood-colored, and ④it has ceramics placed on it. ⑤If a person sits on seat A, in what direction is cabinet B relative to them?
```

**选项：** A: Front-right, B: Rear-right, C: Rear-left, D: Front-left, E: Directly to the right

**正确答案：** `D`  ｜  **模型回答：** `A`

**All Responses：**
```
<think>
1.  **Analyze the User's Question**: The user wants to determine the relative direction of "Cabinet B" from "Seat A" given specific conditions for each.
    *   **Seat A**: Long sofa, green cushions.
    *   **Cabinet B**: Wood-colored, ceramics placed on it.

2.  **Scan the Video for Seat A**:
    *   I need to find a "long sofa" with "green cushions".
    *   0:50 (Living Room): Large blue/grey tufted sofa. Cushions are patterned, light beige/grey. Not explicitly green, but let's keep checking.
    *   2:44 (Porch/Patio): Through a window, we see a white wicker sofa with distinct green square pillows featuring white flowers. This is a very strong match for "long sofa" and "green cushions".
    *   Let's check for other sofas. 3:07 (Bedroom): Bed, armchairs, ottomans. No sofa. 1:28 (Dining): Chairs.
    *   The porch sofa is the best visual match for "green cushions". However, the question asks for the relative position of a cabinet *if a person sits on Seat A*. This usually implies the cabinet is in the same room/visible space.
    *   Let's look for a "Cabinet B" near the porch sofa. The view at 2:44 is through a window from the hallway. We see the sofa outside. Inside the hallway, there is a green console table (2:48). This is not wood-colored. There is no wood cabinet visible on the porch itself.
    *   This suggests "Seat A" might be the living room sofa, and the cushions are described as green (perhaps due to the botanical pattern or lighting, or the surrounding green wallpaper makes them appear so in the context of the question). Let's re-examine the Living Room sofa pillows. At 1:01, they have a leafy pattern. Leaves are green. The wallpaper is green. This is a plausible "green cushions" interpretation, especially if the alternative (porch) has no cabinet.

3.  **Scan the Video for Cabinet B**:
    *   I need a "wood-colored" cabinet with "ceramics placed on it".
    *   1:08 (Living Room): The camera pans to a wooden chest/commode against the wall. On top of it, there is a lamp and a pink ceramic object (looks like a pagoda or jar). On the wall directly above it, there is a collection of about 10 ceramic plates. This fits "wood-colored" and "ceramics placed on it" (or associated with it) very well.
    *   3:08 (Bedroom): There is a large, tall, dark wood china cabinet. On top of it, there is a collection of blue and white ceramic vases/jars. This also fits perfectly.
    *   However, the bedroom has no sofa (only a bed and armchairs).
    *   Therefore, the Living Room is the only space containing both a candidate for Seat A (the sofa, assuming patterned pillows = green) and a strong candidate for Cabinet B (the wooden chest with plates).

4.  **Determine Relative Position in the Living Room**:
    *   **Layout Orientation**:
        *   At 0:50, the camera enters the living room through the front door (pink door, visible at 1:09).
        *   As the camera enters (moving South, if we assume Front=North), the fireplace is on the Left (East) wall.
        *   The sofa is on the Right (West) wall.
        *   Wait, let's verify with the camera pan at 1:08. The camera starts at the sofa and pans *Left* to see the window and then the chest and then the door.
        *   If the sofa is on the West wall, and you look at it (facing West), panning Left means turning to look South. This would look *away* from the Front Door (North). This contradicts seeing the door.
        *   Therefore, the sofa must be on the **East** wall. If you look East at the sofa, panning Left turns you North, towards the Front Door. This matches the video sequence (Sofa -> Window -> Chest -> Door).
        *   So: Sofa is on the East Wall. Front Door and Chest are on the North Wall. Fireplace is on the West Wall.
    *   **Position of Sitter**:
        *   A person sits on Seat A (the sofa on the East wall).
        *   The sofa faces the opposite wall (West, where the fireplace is). So the person is facing **West**.
    *   **Position of Cabinet B**:
        *   The cabinet (wooden chest) is on the North wall (Front wall), adjacent to the door.
    *   **Relative Direction**:
        *   The person faces West.
        *   To the person's Right is North.
        *   To the person's Left is South.
        *   The chest is on the North wall.
        *   Therefore, the chest is to the **Right** of the person.
        *   Is it "Front-Right", "Rear-Right", or "Directly to the Right"?
        *   The chest is on the wall perpendicular to the sofa, in the corner area forward of the sofa (since the sofa is on the side wall and the chest is on the front wall).
        *   Sitter faces West (Front). North is Right. The chest is located North and West relative to the sitter (since it's on the North wall, which spans the width, but spatially it's forward of the sitter's back plane).
        *   In a field of view sense, looking straight ahead (West), the North wall is to the Right. Objects on the adjacent wall forward of the shoulder line are typically described as **Front-Right**.

5.  **Final Verification**:
    *   Seat A: Living room sofa (patterned cushions interpreted as green).
    *   Cabinet B: Wooden chest with plates.
    *   Sitter on sofa faces fireplace. Chest is to the right, near the corner.
    *   Direction: Front-right.

</think>
<answer>A</answer>
```

## ❌ 题目 817（内部 key: 317）
**类别：** home tour ｜ **难度：** Level 3 ｜ **视频：** `ht14`

**题目：**
```
On a table C: ①There are four cup-like objects placed, and ②two of them are green. The main color of the remaining two is A. Another chair B satisfies: ③There are multiple identical ones, and ④the color of the seat cushion is A. ⑤If a person sits on this chair, in what direction is table C relative to them?
```

**选项：** A: Front-right, B: Rear-left, C: Rear-right, D: Front-left, E: Directly ahead

**正确答案：** `D`  ｜  **模型回答：** `E`

**All Responses：**
```
The reasoning for the answer is as follows:

1.  **Identify "Chair B" and "Color A":**
    *   The video displays several types of chairs. We are looking for "multiple identical ones" where the cushion color determines "Color A".
    *   At 1:30, there are four identical dining chairs with **green** cushions. If these were Chair B, Color A would be green.
    *   At 2:16, there are two identical chairs with **blue** cushions in the hallway area, flanking the yellow pantry. If these were Chair B, Color A would be blue.
    *   At 3:08, there are two identical chairs with **blue** cushions in the bedroom.

2.  **Identify "Table C":**
    *   We need to find a table with four cup-like objects: two green and two of Color A.
    *   If Color A is **Green** (Dining Chairs): We need 4 green cups. The dining table (1:30) has purple glasses, so this doesn't match.
    *   If Color A is **Blue** (Hallway/Bedroom Chairs): We need 2 green cups and 2 blue cups.
    *   Let's examine the tables near the blue chairs. In the hallway (2:38), directly across from the blue chairs, there is a wooden console table. On this table, we can see a **blue ceramic pot** (Color A) and a **green glass hurricane/vase**. While distinct "four cups" might be obscured or represented by these decorative objects (often arranged in pairs in design), this is the only table featuring both Blue and Green objects corresponding to the chair color.

3.  **Determine the Direction:**
    *   Assuming Chair B is one of the **Blue Chairs** in the hallway (2:16) and Table C is the **Console Table** (2:38).
    *   The blue chairs are placed against the wall on one side of the hallway.
    *   The console table is placed against the wall on the opposite side of the hallway.
    *   If a person sits on Chair B, they face across the hallway.
    *   Therefore, Table C is located **directly ahead** of them.

<answer>E</answer>
```

## ❌ 题目 818（内部 key: 318）
**类别：** home tour ｜ **难度：** Level 2 ｜ **视频：** `ht14`

**题目：**
```
①The main color in room A is yellow. ②If a person stands outside this room facing it, ③what is the background color of the topmost painting on the wall to their front-right?
```

**选项：** A: Black, B: Red, C: White, D: Blue, E: Green

**正确答案：** `C`  ｜  **模型回答：** `D`

**All Responses：**
```
The room described as having yellow as its main color is the **hosting closet (or pantry)** shown around the 2:17 mark, which features bright yellow shelves and walls.

If a person stands outside this room facing it (from the kitchen), the wall to their **front-right** is the wall adjacent to the closet, where a console table and a chair are located. On this wall, there are two framed paintings of bunnies stacked vertically. The question asks for the background color of the **topmost painting**.

Looking at the video (specifically around 2:38), the painting has a white outline of a bunny on a dark background. Given the strong blue and white theme throughout the house (blue patterned wallpaper, blue chair cushion, blue porcelain), and the deep navy hue of the painting's background visible in the light, the color is **blue**.

<answer>D</answer>
```
